✅ High-Risk Client / Fraud Family – Option A Status
You now have Option A (n8n JSON) for this family:

PT_Risk_ClientHighRiskFlagged

Real-time alerts when a client becomes high/critical risk

Optional backend “mark alerted” hook

PT_Risk_FraudAlertCreated

Real-time alerts on fraud alerts

Optional auto-routing of disputes to trust_safety

PT_Risk_DailyRiskSummary

Daily snapshot of risk bands + new high/critical + fraud alerts

That completes this family at the automation layer.

If you’re ready, I’ll proceed to the next family under Option A (Booking & Job Lifecycle Comms).


proceed to the next family

Alright, on to the next family in Option A:

Family – Booking & Job Lifecycle Communications
(all n8n workflows as JSON, import-ready)

This family covers all the core communications from the moment a client books → cleaner assigned → cleaner arrives → job finished → client approves.

I’ll give you 7 workflows:

PT_Jobs_BookingCreated – confirmation to client

PT_Jobs_BookingReminder24h – 24h reminder before job

PT_Jobs_BookingReminder2h – 2h reminder before job

PT_Jobs_CleanerAssigned – notify client & cleaner

PT_Jobs_CleanerCheckin – notify client when cleaner arrives

PT_Jobs_JobCompletedAwaitingApproval – “approve or dispute” email

PT_Jobs_ApprovalReminder – remind client before dispute window expires

PT_Jobs_JobApproved – final confirmation to both sides

(7+8 are tightly related; I’ll keep them compact.)

You can adjust event names and payload fields to match your actual backend events.

1️⃣ PT_Jobs_BookingCreated
Goal:
When a booking is created, send the client booking confirmation (with date/time, address, cleaner placeholder or TBD).

Assumed event:

event_name = "booking.created"

Payload example:

{
  "event_name": "booking.created",
  "payload": {
    "job_id": "job_123",
    "client_id": "cli_123",
    "client_email": "client@example.com",
    "scheduled_start": "2025-01-05T14:00:00Z",
    "duration_hours": 3,
    "address_line": "123 Main St",
    "city": "Austin",
    "timezone": "America/Chicago"
  }
}
n8n JSON
{
  "name": "PT_Jobs_BookingCreated",
  "nodes": [
    {
      "id": "Webhook_BookingCreated",
      "name": "Events Webhook (Jobs)",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.webhook",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [260, 300],
      "parameters": {
        "httpMethod": "POST",
        "path": "events-jobs",
        "options": {
          "ignoreBots": true
        }
      }
    },
    {
      "id": "If_BookingCreated",
      "name": "Filter booking.created",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.if",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [520, 300],
      "parameters": {
        "conditions": {
          "string": [
            {
              "value1": "={{$json[\"event_name\"]}}",
              "operation": "equal",
              "value2": "booking.created"
            }
          ]
        }
      }
    },
    {
      "id": "Email_BookingConfirm",
      "name": "Email: Booking Confirmation",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.httpRequest",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [800, 300],
      "parameters": {
        "url": "https://api.sendgrid.com/v3/mail/send",
        "method": "POST",
        "authentication": "headerAuth",
        "headerParametersJson": "={\"Authorization\": \"Bearer \" + $env.SENDGRID_API_KEY}",
        "jsonParameters": true,
        "bodyParametersJson": "={\n  \"personalizations\": [\n    {\n      \"to\": [ { \"email\": $json.payload.client_email || \"\" } ],\n      \"subject\": \"Your PureTask cleaning is booked\"\n    }\n  ],\n  \"from\": { \"email\": $env.ALERT_EMAIL_FROM },\n  \"content\": [\n    {\n      \"type\": \"text/plain\",\n      \"value\": \"Hi,\\n\\nYour cleaning has been booked.\\n\\nJob ID: \" + $json.payload.job_id + \"\\nDate & time: \" + ($json.payload.scheduled_start || \"\") + \" (\" + ($json.payload.timezone || \"\") + \")\\nDuration: \" + ($json.payload.duration_hours || 0) + \" hours\\nAddress: \" + ($json.payload.address_line || \"\") + \", \" + ($json.payload.city || \"\") + \"\\n\\nYou can view or manage this booking in your PureTask account.\\n\\n— PureTask\\n\"\n    }\n  ]\n}"
      }
    }
  ],
  "connections": {
    "Events Webhook (Jobs)": {
      "main": [
        [
          {
            "node": "Filter booking.created",
            "type": "main",
            "index": 0
          }
        ]
      ]
    },
    "Filter booking.created": {
      "main": [
        [
          {
            "node": "Email: Booking Confirmation",
            "type": "main",
            "index": 0
          }
        ]
      ]
    }
  },
  "active": false
}

]

4️⃣ PT_Jobs_CleanerAssigned
Goal:
When a cleaner is assigned to a job, notify:

Client → “Cleaner assigned”

Cleaner → “New job assigned to you”

Assumed event:

event_name = "job.assigned"

Payload example:

{
  "event_name": "job.assigned",
  "payload": {
    "job_id": "job_123",
    "client_email": "client@example.com",
    "cleaner_email": "cleaner@example.com",
    "cleaner_name": "Alex",
    "scheduled_start": "2025-01-05T14:00:00Z",
    "timezone": "America/Chicago"
  }
}

        "bodyParametersJson": "={\n  \"personalizations\": [\n    {\n      \"to\": [ { \"email\": $json.payload.client_email || \"\" } ],\n      \"subject\": \"Your PureTask cleaner has arrived\"\n    }\n  ],\n  \"from\": { \"email\": $env.ALERT_EMAIL_FROM },\n  \"content\": [\n    {\n      \"type\": \"text/plain\",\n      \"value\": \"Hi,\\n\\nYour cleaner \" + ($json.payload.cleaner_name || \"\") + \" has arrived and checked in.\\n\\nIf anything looks off, you can chat with them in the app.\\n\\n— PureTask\\n\"\n    }\n  ]\n}"
      }
    }
  ],
  "connections": {
    "Events Webhook (Checkins)": {
      "main": [
        [
          {
            "node": "Filter job.cleaner_checked_in",
            "type": "main",
            "index": 0
          }
        ]
      ]
    },
    "Filter job.cleaner_checked_in": {
      "main": [
        [
          {
            "node": "Email: Cleaner Arrived",
            "type": "main",
            "index": 0
          }
        ]
      ]
    }
  },
  "active": false
}
6️⃣ PT_Jobs_JobCompletedAwaitingApproval
Goal:
When cleaner submits job as completed (photos + notes uploaded), send the client:

“Review and approve or dispute this job.”

Assumed event:

event_name = "job.awaiting_approval"

Payload example:

{
  "event_name": "job.awaiting_approval",
  "payload": {
    "job_id": "job_123",
    "client_email": "client@example.com",
    "approval_url": "https://app.puretask.com/jobs/job_123/approve",
    "expires_at": "2025-01-06T14:00:00Z"
  }
}
n8n JSON

  "active": false

7️⃣ PT_Jobs_ApprovalReminder
Goal:
Before the dispute window expires (e.g. 24h after completion, or 12h before auto-approve), remind client to approve/dispute.

Assumed backend endpoint:

GET /internal/reminders/jobs-awaiting-approval

Returns a list of jobs:

[
  {
    "job_id": "job_123",
    "client_email": "client@example.com",
    "approval_url": "https://app.puretask.com/jobs/job_123/approve",
    "expires_at": "2025-01-06T14:00:00Z",
    "hours_until_expiry": 12
  }
]
n8n JSON

8️⃣ PT_Jobs_JobApproved
Goal:
When a job is approved (client approves or auto-approval), send:

Client → final receipt/thanks

Cleaner → “job approved, earnings updated”

Assumed event:

event_name = "job.approved"

Payload example:

{
  "event_name": "job.approved",
  "payload": {
    "job_id": "job_123",
    "client_email": "client@example.com",
    "cleaner_email": "cleaner@example.com",
    "amount_cents": 12000,
    "credits_spent": 1200
  }
}

      }
    },

        "url": "https://api.sendgrid.com/v3/mail/send",
        "method": "POST",

✅ Booking & Job Lifecycle Comms – Option A Status
For this family, you now have importable n8n workflows for:

PT_Jobs_BookingCreated

PT_Jobs_BookingReminder24h

PT_Jobs_BookingReminder2h

PT_Jobs_CleanerAssigned

PT_Jobs_CleanerCheckin

PT_Jobs_JobCompletedAwaitingApproval

PT_Jobs_ApprovalReminder

PT_Jobs_JobApproved

That covers the entire core job communication arc:
Book → remind → assign → arrive → complete → approve.

If you’re ready to keep going with Option A, just say:

“Proceed to the next family.”


proceed

Nice, rolling on with Option A to the next family:

Family – Rescheduling Workflows (Comms + Orchestration)

Backend already handles:

Time buckets (>48h, 24–48h, <24h)

Reason codes

Reasonableness checks

Flexibility penalties

Policy outcomes

n8n’s job here: tell humans what’s happening, based on backend events.

I’ll give you 4 workflows:

PT_Reschedule_RequestCreated – notify the other party when a reschedule is requested

PT_Reschedule_RequestResolved – notify both sides when it’s approved/declined

PT_Reschedule_PendingReminder – remind when a reschedule request is still pending action

PT_Reschedule_ReasonableOverrideAlert – alert ops if backend flags something “reasonable but blocked / edge-case”

You can tweak event names to your actual backend; I’m following your spec naming style.

1️⃣ Workflow: PT_Reschedule_RequestCreated
Goal

When a reschedule is requested (by client or cleaner), notify the other side:

If client requests → notify cleaner

If cleaner requests → notify client

Assumed event:

event_name = "reschedule.requested"

Payload example:

{
  "event_name": "reschedule.requested",
  "payload": {
    "reschedule_id": "rs_123",
    "job_id": "job_123",
    "requested_by": "client",          // or "cleaner"
    "requested_by_id": "cli_123",
    "target_party": "cleaner",         // or "client"
    "target_email": "cleaner@example.com",
    "old_start": "2025-01-05T14:00:00Z",
    "new_start": "2025-01-06T10:00:00Z",
    "timezone": "America/Chicago",
    "reason_code": "schedule_conflict",
    "reason_text": "Running late from work",
    "time_bucket": ">48h"              // or "24-48h", "<24h"
  }
}
n8n JSON
{
  "name": "PT_Reschedule_RequestCreated",
  "nodes": [
    {
      "id": "Webhook_RescheduleRequested",
      "name": "Events Webhook (Reschedule)",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.webhook",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [260, 300],
      "parameters": {
        "httpMethod": "POST",
        "path": "events-reschedule",
        "options": {
          "ignoreBots": true
        }
      }
    },
    {
      "id": "If_RescheduleRequested",
      "name": "Filter reschedule.requested",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.if",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [520, 300],
      "parameters": {
        "conditions": {
          "string": [
            {
              "value1": "={{$json[\"event_name\"]}}",
              "operation": "equal",
              "value2": "reschedule.requested"
            }
          ]
        }
      }
    },
    {
      "id": "Email_TargetParty",
      "name": "Email: Reschedule Request → Target",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.httpRequest",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [800, 300],
      "parameters": {
        "url": "https://api.sendgrid.com/v3/mail/send",
        "method": "POST",
        "authentication": "headerAuth",
        "headerParametersJson": "={\"Authorization\": \"Bearer \" + $env.SENDGRID_API_KEY}",
        "jsonParameters": true,
        "bodyParametersJson": "={\n  \"personalizations\": [\n    {\n      \"to\": [ { \"email\": $json.payload.target_email || \"\" } ],\n      \"subject\": \"Reschedule request for your PureTask job\"\n    }\n  ],\n  \"from\": { \"email\": $env.ALERT_EMAIL_FROM },\n  \"content\": [\n    {\n      \"type\": \"text/plain\",\n      \"value\": \"Hi,\\n\\nThere is a reschedule request for one of your jobs.\\n\\nJob ID: \" + $json.payload.job_id + \"\\nRequested by: \" + ($json.payload.requested_by || \"\") + \"\\nCurrent time: \" + ($json.payload.old_start || \"\") + \" (\" + ($json.payload.timezone || \"\") + \")\\nRequested new time: \" + ($json.payload.new_start || \"\") + \" (\" + ($json.payload.timezone || \"\") + \")\\nReason: \" + ($json.payload.reason_text || $json.payload.reason_code || \"(not provided)\") + \"\\n\\nPlease open your PureTask app to accept or decline this request.\\n\\n— PureTask\\n\"\n    }\n  ]\n}"
      }
    }
  ],
  "connections": {
    "Events Webhook (Reschedule)": {
      "main": [
        [
          {
            "node": "Filter reschedule.requested",
            "type": "main",
            "index": 0
          }
        ]
      ]
    },
    "Filter reschedule.requested": {
      "main": [
        [
          {
            "node": "Email: Reschedule Request → Target",
            "type": "main",
            "index": 0
          }
        ]
      ]
    }
  },
  "active": false
}
2️⃣ Workflow: PT_Reschedule_RequestResolved
Goal

When a reschedule request is approved or declined, notify:

Both client and cleaner with the outcome

Use one workflow that branches on status

Assumed event:

event_name = "reschedule.resolved"

Payload example:

{
  "event_name": "reschedule.resolved",
  "payload": {
    "reschedule_id": "rs_123",
    "job_id": "job_123",
    "status": "approved",          // or "declined"
    "old_start": "2025-01-05T14:00:00Z",
    "new_start": "2025-01-06T10:00:00Z",
    "timezone": "America/Chicago",
    "resolved_by": "cleaner",      // or "client" or "system"
    "client_email": "client@example.com",
    "cleaner_email": "cleaner@example.com",
    "reason_text": "Running late from work",
    "note": "Approved via app"
  }
}
n8n JSON
{
  "name": "PT_Reschedule_RequestResolved",
  "nodes": [
    {
      "id": "Webhook_RescheduleResolved",
      "name": "Events Webhook (Reschedule Resolved)",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.webhook",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [260, 300],
      "parameters": {
        "httpMethod": "POST",
        "path": "events-reschedule-resolved",
        "options": {
          "ignoreBots": true
        }
      }
    },
    {
      "id": "If_RescheduleResolved",
      "name": "Filter reschedule.resolved",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.if",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [520, 300],
      "parameters": {
        "conditions": {
          "string": [
            {
              "value1": "={{$json[\"event_name\"]}}",
              "operation": "equal",
              "value2": "reschedule.resolved"
            }
          ]
        }
      }
    },
    {
      "id": "Switch_Status",
      "name": "Switch: Approved vs Declined",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.switch",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [780, 300],
      "parameters": {
        "propertyName": "={{$json.payload.status}}",
        "rules": [
          { "operation": "equal", "value": "approved" },
          { "operation": "equal", "value": "declined" }
        ]
      }
    },
    {
      "id": "Email_ClientApproved",
      "name": "Email Client: Reschedule Approved",

        "url": "https://api.sendgrid.com/v3/mail/send",
        "method": "POST",
        "authentication": "headerAuth",
        "headerParametersJson": "={\"Authorization\": \"Bearer \" + $env.SENDGRID_API_KEY}",
        "jsonParameters": true,
        "bodyParametersJson": "={\n \"personalizations\": [\n   {\n     \"to\": [ { \"email\": $json.payload.client_email || \"\" } ],\n     \"subject\": \"Your PureTask reschedule has been approved\"\n   }\n ],\n \"from\": { \"email\": $env.ALERT_EMAIL_FROM },\n \"content\": [\n   {\n     \"type\": \"text/plain\",\n     \"value\": \"Hi,\\n\\nYour reschedule request has been approved.\\n\\nJob ID: \" + $json.payload.job_id + \"\\nNew time: \" + ($json.payload.new_start || \"\") + \" (\" + ($json.payload.timezone || \"\") + \")\\n\\nReason: \" + ($json.payload.reason_text || \"(not provided)\") + \"\\n\\n— PureTask\\n\"\n   }\n ]\n}"
      }
    },
    {
      "id": "Email_CleanerApproved",
      "name": "Email Cleaner: Reschedule Approved",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.httpRequest",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [1040, 280],
      "parameters": {
        "url": "https://api.sendgrid.com/v3/mail/send",
        "method": "POST",
        "authentication": "headerAuth",
        "headerParametersJson": "={\"Authorization\": \"Bearer \" + $env.SENDGRID_API_KEY}",
        "jsonParameters": true,
        "bodyParametersJson": "={\n \"personalizations\": [\n   {\n     \"to\": [ { \"email\": $json.payload.cleaner_email || \"\" } ],\n     \"subject\": \"Job reschedule approved\"\n   }\n ],\n \"from\": { \"email\": $env.ALERT_EMAIL_FROM },\n \"content\": [\n   {\n     \"type\": \"text/plain\",\n     \"value\": \"Hi,\\n\\nA reschedule for one of your jobs has been approved.\\n\\nJob ID: \" + $json.payload.job_id + \"\\nNew time: \" + ($json.payload.new_start || \"\") + \" (\" + ($json.payload.timezone || \"\") + \")\\n\\nPlease check your schedule in the PureTask app.\\n\\n— PureTask\\n\"\n   }\n ]\n}"
      }
    },
    {
      "id": "Email_ClientDeclined",
      "name": "Email Client: Reschedule Declined",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.httpRequest",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [1040, 420],
      "parameters": {
        "url": "https://api.sendgrid.com/v3/mail/send",
        "method": "POST",
        "authentication": "headerAuth",
        "headerParametersJson": "={\"Authorization\": \"Bearer \" + $env.SENDGRID_API_KEY}",
        "jsonParameters": true,
        "bodyParametersJson": "={\n \"personalizations\": [\n   {\n     \"to\": [ { \"email\": $json.payload.client_email || \"\" } ],\n     \"subject\": \"Your PureTask reschedule was not approved\"\n   }\n ],\n \"from\": { \"email\": $env.ALERT_EMAIL_FROM },\n \"content\": [\n   {\n     \"type\": \"text/plain\",\n     \"value\": \"Hi,\\n\\nYour reschedule request could not be approved. The job currently remains at its original time.\\n\\nJob ID: \" + $json.payload.job_id + \"\\nOriginal time: \" + ($json.payload.old_start || \"\") + \" (\" + ($json.payload.timezone || \"\") + \")\\n\\nIf you still need to change this booking, please open your PureTask account to explore options.\\n\\n— PureTask\\n\"\n   }\n ]\n}"
      }
    },
    {
      "id": "Email_CleanerDeclined",
      "name": "Email Cleaner: Reschedule Declined (FYI)",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.httpRequest",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [1040, 520],
      "parameters": {
        "url": "https://api.sendgrid.com/v3/mail/send",
        "method": "POST",
        "authentication": "headerAuth",
        "headerParametersJson": "={\"Authorization\": \"Bearer \" + $env.SENDGRID_API_KEY}",
        "jsonParameters": true,
        "bodyParametersJson": "={\n \"personalizations\": [\n   {\n     \"to\": [ { \"email\": $json.payload.cleaner_email || \"\" } ],\n     \"subject\": \"Reschedule request not approved\"\n   }\n ],\n \"from\": { \"email\": $env.ALERT_EMAIL_FROM },\n \"content\": [\n   {\n     \"type\": \"text/plain\",\n     \"value\": \"Hi,\\n\\nA reschedule request on one of your jobs was not approved. 3️⃣ Workflow: PT_Reschedule_PendingReminder
Goal

If a reschedule request is still pending after X hours, remind the target party to act:

Example: remind after 4 hours, then maybe again at 12 hours

Assumed backend endpoint:

GET /internal/reminders/reschedules-pending?min_age_hours=4

Returns an array:

[
  {
    "reschedule_id": "rs_123",
    "job_id": "job_123",
    "target_email": "cleaner@example.com",
    "target_role": "cleaner",
    "requested_by_role": "client",
    "old_start": "2025-01-05T14:00:00Z",
    "new_start": "2025-01-06T10:00:00Z",
    "timezone": "America/Chicago",
    "age_hours": 5
  }
]
n8n JSON
{
  "name": "PT_Reschedule_PendingReminder",
  "nodes": [
    {
      "id": "Cron_PendingReschedules",
      "name": "Every 2 hours",

      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [260, 300],
      "parameters": {
        "triggerTimes": [
          { "hour": 0, "minute": 0 }
        ],
        "interval": 2,
        "unit": "hours"

      "parameters": {
        "url": "https://backend.yourdomain.com/internal/reminders/reschedules-pending?min_age_hours=4",
        "method": "GET",
        "jsonParameters": true
      }
    },
    {
      "id": "Split_PendingReschedules",

4️⃣ Workflow: PT_Reschedule_ReasonableOverrideAlert (optional but powerful)
Goal

Backend sometimes flags “this request looks reasonable but would be blocked by policy” (e.g. edge-case time buckets, or repeated issues with same client/cleaner). When that happens:

Alert support/ops to manually review & possibly override

This is your “human escape hatch” for the reschedule engine

Assumed event:

event_name = "reschedule.reasonable_override_required"

Payload example:

{
  "event_name": "reschedule.reasonable_override_required",
  "payload": {
    "reschedule_id": "rs_123",
    "job_id": "job_123",
    "client_id": "cli_123",
    "cleaner_id": "clr_123",
    "reason_text": "Child got sick",
    "time_bucket": "<24h",
    "recommended_action": "waive_fee_and_allow",
    "details": { "past_flexibility": "high", "no_shows": 0 }
  }
}
n8n JSON
{
  "name": "PT_Reschedule_ReasonableOverrideAlert",
  "nodes": [
    {
      "id": "Webhook_ReasonableOverride",
      "name": "Events Webhook (Reschedule Overrides)",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.webhook",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [260, 300],
      "parameters": {
        "httpMethod": "POST",
        "path": "events-reschedule-overrides",
        "options": {
          "ignoreBots": true
        }
      }
    },
    {
      "id": "If_ReasonableOverride",
      "name": "Filter reschedule.reasonable_override_required",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.if",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [520, 300],
      "parameters": {
        "conditions": {
          "string": [
            {
              "value1": "={{$json[\"event_name\"]}}",
              "operation": "equal",
              "value2": "reschedule.reasonable_override_required"
            }
          ]
        }
      }
    },
    {
      "id": "Slack_OverrideAlert",
      "name": "Slack: Reschedule Override Alert",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.httpRequest",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [800, 260],
      "parameters": {
        "url": "={{$env.ALERT_SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL}}",
        "method": "POST",
        "jsonParameters": true,
        "bodyParametersJson": "={\n \"text\": \"⚖️ Reschedule override recommended.\\nJob: `\" + $json.payload.job_id + \"`\\nReschedule: `\" + $json.payload.reschedule_id + \"`\\nClient: `\" + $json.payload.client_id + \"`\\nCleaner: `\" + $json.payload.cleaner_id + \"`\\nTime bucket: \" + ($json.payload.time_bucket || \"\") + \"\\nReason: \" + ($json.payload.reason_text || \"(none)\") + \"\\nRecommended: \" + ($json.payload.recommended_action || \"review\") + \"\\n\"\n}"
      }
    },
    {
      "id": "Email_OverrideAlert",
      "name": "Email: Reschedule Override Alert",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.httpRequest",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [800, 420],
      "parameters": {
        "url": "https://api.sendgrid.com/v3/mail/send",
        "method": "POST",
        "authentication": "headerAuth",
        "headerParametersJson": "={\"Authorization\": \"Bearer \" + $env.SENDGRID_API_KEY}",
        "jsonParameters": true,
        "bodyParametersJson": "={\n \"personalizations\": [\n   {\n     \"to\": [ { \"email\": $env.ALERT_EMAIL_TO } ],\n     \"subject\": \"[PureTask] Reschedule override recommended for job \" + $json.payload.job_id\n   }\n ],\n \"from\": { \"email\": $env.ALERT_EMAIL_FROM },\n \"content\": [\n   {\n     \"type\": \"text/plain\",\n     \"value\": \"A reschedule appears reasonable but conflicts with standard policy and may require manual override.\\n\\nJob ID: \" + $json.payload.job_id + \"\\nReschedule ID: \" + $json.payload.reschedule_id + \"\\nClient ID: \" + $json.payload.client_id + \"\\nCleaner ID: \" + $json.payload.cleaner_id + \"\\nTime bucket: \" + ($json.payload.time_bucket || \"\") + \"\\nReason: \" + ($json.payload.reason_text || \"(none)\") + \"\\nRecommended action: \" + ($json.payload.recommended_action || \"review\") + \"\\nDetails: \" + JSON.stringify($json.payload.details || {}, null, 2) + \"\\n\"\n   }\n ]\n}"
      }
    }
  ],
  "connections": {
    "Events Webhook (Reschedule Overrides)": {
      "main": [
        [
          {
            "node": "Filter reschedule.reasonable_override_required",
            "type": "main",
            "index": 0
          }
        ]
      ]
    },
    "Filter reschedule.reasonable_override_required": {
      "main": [
        [
          {

✅ Rescheduling Family – Option A Status
You now have importable workflows for:

PT_Reschedule_RequestCreated

PT_Reschedule_RequestResolved

PT_Reschedule_PendingReminder

PT_Reschedule_ReasonableOverrideAlert

These cover:

Real-time notifications for new reschedule requests

Outcome notifications for approval/decline

Time-based nudges when requests sit too long

A human override hook for tricky “reasonable but blocked” cases

If you’d like to keep going under Option A, the next family in the chain would be:

Cancellation Workflows (fees / grace / lock-window / no-shows)

If you want that next, just say “proceed” again and I’ll generate the cancellation family JSON.

Continuing Option A.

Next Family — Cancellation Workflows (Policies, Fees, No-Shows, Comms)
This family handles all cancellation-related human notifications + ops alerts, while your backend enforces policy (lock window, grace cancels, fees, no-shows, refunds).

I’ll deliver 6 import-ready n8n workflows:

PT_Cancel_PreviewRequested – optional UX assist (fee preview confirmation)

PT_Cancel_Confirmed – notify parties after cancellation is finalized

PT_Cancel_GraceUsed – notify client when a grace cancel is consumed

PT_Cancel_LockWindowBlocked – notify requester when cancellation is blocked

PT_NoShow_Detected – notify + compensate per policy

PT_Cancel_OpsAlert_EdgeCase – ops alert for unusual or repeated cancels

1️⃣ PT_Cancel_PreviewRequested (Optional but useful)
Goal: When a user requests a cancellation preview (fees/refund), confirm details by email (optional; many apps skip this).

Event: cancellation.previewed

{
  "name": "PT_Cancel_PreviewRequested",
  "nodes": [
    {
      "id": "Webhook_Preview",
      "name": "Events Webhook (Cancel Preview)",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.webhook",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [260, 300],
      "parameters": { "httpMethod": "POST", "path": "events-cancel-preview" }
    },
    {
      "id": "If_Preview",
      "name": "Filter cancellation.previewed",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.if",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [520, 300],
      "parameters": {
        "conditions": { "string": [{ "value1": "={{$json.event_name}}", "operation": "equal", "value2": "cancellation.previewed" }] }
      }
    },
    {
      "id": "Email_Preview",
      "name": "Email: Cancellation Preview",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.httpRequest",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [800, 300],
      "parameters": {
        "url": "https://api.sendgrid.com/v3/mail/send",
        "method": "POST",
        "authentication": "headerAuth",
        "headerParametersJson": "={\"Authorization\":\"Bearer \"+$env.SENDGRID_API_KEY}",
        "jsonParameters": true,
        "bodyParametersJson": "={\"personalizations\":[{\"to\":[{\"email\":$json.payload.email}],\"subject\":\"Cancellation preview\"}],\"from\":{\"email\":$env.ALERT_EMAIL_FROM},\"content\":[{\"type\":\"text/plain\",\"value\":\"Job: \"+$json.payload.job_id+\"\\nEstimated refund: \"+$json.payload.refund_credits+\" credits\\nFee: \"+$json.payload.fee_percent+\"%\\nLock window: \"+$json.payload.locked}\"}]}"
      }
    }
  ],
  "connections": {

Proceeding ✅

Next Family — Payouts & Financial Ops Workflows (Option A: n8n JSON)
This family is specifically the ops layer around payouts (holds, reversals, retries, weekly summaries). Your backend already handles the ledger + payout engine; n8n does alerts + routing + summaries.

Delivering 6 workflows:

PT_Payouts_WeeklyRunStarted

PT_Payouts_PayoutCreated

PT_Payouts_PayoutFailed

PT_Payouts_PayoutRetryExhausted

PT_Payouts_PayoutHoldOrReverse

PT_Payouts_WeeklySummary

1️⃣ PT_Payouts_WeeklyRunStarted
Event: payouts.weekly.started
Goal: Alert ops/finance that weekly payout batch started.

{
  "name": "PT_Payouts_WeeklyRunStarted",
  "nodes": [
    {
      "id": "Webhook",
      "name": "Events Webhook (Payouts)",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.webhook",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [260, 300],
      "parameters": { "httpMethod": "POST", "path": "events-payouts-weekly-started" }
    },
    {
      "id": "If",
      "name": "Filter payouts.weekly.started",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.if",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [520, 300],
      "parameters": {
        "conditions": { "string": [{ "value1": "={{$json.event_name}}", "operation": "equal", "value2": "payouts.weekly.started" }] }
      }
    },
    {
      "id": "Slack",
      "name": "Slack: Weekly Payouts Started",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.httpRequest",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [800, 300],
      "parameters": {
        "url": "={{$env.ALERT_SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL}}",
        "method": "POST",
        "jsonParameters": true,
        "bodyParametersJson": "={\"text\":\"💰 Weekly payouts batch STARTED. Run ID: `\"+($json.payload.run_id||\"n/a\")+\"`\"}"
      }
    }
  ],
  "connections": {
    "Events Webhook (Payouts)": { "main": [[{ "node": "Filter payouts.weekly.started", "type": "main", "index": 0 }]] },
    "Filter payouts.weekly.started": { "main": [[{ "node": "Slack: Weekly Payouts Started", "type": "main", "index": 0 }]] }
  },
  "active": false
}

      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [520, 300],
      "parameters": {
        "conditions": {
          "multi": [
            { "conditions": { "string": [{ "value1": "={{$json.event_name}}", "operation": "equal", "value2": "payout.hold_set" }] } },
            { "conditions": { "string": [{ "value1": "={{$json.event_name}}", "operation": "equal", "value2": "payout.reversed" }] } }
          ],
          "combineOperation": "any"
        }
      }
    },

6️⃣ PT_Payouts_WeeklySummary
Cron: weekly (or daily during early launch)
Goal: send ops/finance totals: total payouts, failures, holds, reversals, top 10 largest payouts.

Assumed backend endpoint:
GET https://backend.yourdomain.com/admin/payouts/weekly-summary

Returns e.g.

{
  "week":"2025-W01",
  "total_payouts":120,
  "total_amount_cents":3450000,
  "failed":3,
  "held":2,
  "reversed":1
}
{
  "name": "PT_Payouts_WeeklySummary",
  "nodes": [
    {
      "id": "Cron",
      "name": "Weekly Monday 09:30",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.cron",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [260, 300],
      "parameters": { "triggerTimes": [{ "weekday": "monday", "hour": 9, "minute": 30 }] }
    },
    {
      "id": "Get",
      "name": "Backend: Weekly Payout Summary",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.httpRequest",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [520, 300],
      "parameters": { "url": "https://backend.yourdomain.com/admin/payouts/weekly-summary", "method": "GET", "jsonParameters": true }
    },
    {
      "id": "Build",
      "name": "Build Summary Text",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.function",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [780, 300],
      "parameters": {
        "functionCode": "const amt = (($json.total_amount_cents||0)/100).toFixed(2);\nconst lines = [\n`💰 Weekly payouts summary (${($json.week||'n/a')})`,\n`Total payouts: ${$json.total_payouts||0}`,\n`Total amount: $${amt}`,\n`Failed: ${$json.failed||0}`,\n`Held: ${$json.held||0}`,\n`Reversed: ${$json.reversed||0}`\n];\nreturn [{json:{text:lines.join('\\n')}}];"
      }
    },
    {
      "id": "Slack",
      "name": "Slack: Weekly Summary",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.httpRequest",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [1040, 260],
      "parameters": {
        "url": "={{$env.ALERT_SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL}}",
        "method": "POST",
        "jsonParameters": true,
        "bodyParametersJson": "={\"text\":$json.text}"
      }
    },
    {
      "id": "Email",
      "name": "Email: Weekly Summary",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.httpRequest",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [1040, 420],
      "parameters": {
        "url": "https://api.sendgrid.com/v3/mail/send",
        "method": "POST",
        "authentication": "headerAuth",
        "headerParametersJson": "={\"Authorization\":\"Bearer \"+$env.SENDGRID_API_KEY}",
        "jsonParameters": true,
        "bodyParametersJson": "={\"personalizations\":[{\"to\":[{\"email\":$env.ALERT_EMAIL_TO}],\"subject\":\"[PureTask] Weekly payouts summary\"}],\"from\":{\"email\":$env.ALERT_EMAIL_FROM},\"content\":[{\"type\":\"text/plain\",\"value\":$json.text}]}"
      }
    }
  ],
  "connections": {
    "Weekly Monday 09:30": { "main": [[{ "node": "Backend: Weekly Payout Summary", "type": "main", "index": 0 }]] },
    "Backend: Weekly Payout Summary": { "main": [[{ "node": "Build Summary Text", "type": "main", "index": 0 }]] },
    "Build Summary Text": { "main": [[{ "node": "Slack: Weekly Summary", "type": "main", "index": 0 }, { "node": "Email: Weekly Summary", "type": "main", "index": 0 }]] }
  },
  "active": false
}

Proceeding ✅

Next Family — Messaging + Support Ops Workflows (Option A: n8n JSON)
This family automates support intake, dispute routing alerts, SLA reminders, escalation, and daily ops summaries. Backend is system-of-record; n8n is the notification + routing glue.

Delivering 7 workflows:

PT_Support_TicketCreated

PT_Support_TicketAssignedOrRouted

PT_Support_TicketSlaBreachReminder

PT_Support_DisputeCreated

PT_Support_DisputeRouted

PT_Support_HighPriorityMessageFlagged

PT_Support_DailyOpsSummary

1️⃣ PT_Support_TicketCreated
Event: support.ticket.created
Goal: confirm to user + alert support channel.

{
  "name": "PT_Support_TicketCreated",
  "nodes": [
    { "id": "Webhook", "name": "Events Webhook (Support)", "type": "n8n-nodes-base.webhook", "typeVersion": 1, "position": [260, 300], "parameters": { "httpMethod": "POST", "path": "events-support-ticket-created" } },
    { "id": "If", "name": "Filter support.ticket.created", "type": "n8n-nodes-base.if", "typeVersion": 1, "position": [520, 300], "parameters": { "conditions": { "string": [{ "value1": "={{$json.event_name}}", "operation": "equal", "value2": "support.ticket.created" }] } } },
    {
      "id": "Slack",
      "name": "Slack: New Support Ticket",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.httpRequest",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [800, 220],
      "parameters": {
        "url": "={{$env.ALERT_SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL}}",
        "method": "POST",
        "jsonParameters": true,
        "bodyParametersJson": "={\"text\":\"🎫 New support ticket: `\"+$json.payload.ticket_id+\"`\\nFrom: \"+($json.payload.user_id||\"unknown\")+\" (\"+($json.payload.user_role||\"?\")+\")\\nPriority: \"+($json.payload.priority||\"normal\")+\"\\nSubject: \"+($json.payload.subject||\"(none)\")}"
      }
    },
    {
      "id": "EmailUser",
      "name": "Email: Ticket Confirmation (User)",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.httpRequest",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [800, 420],
      "parameters": {
        "url": "https://api.sendgrid.com/v3/mail/send",
        "method": "POST",
        "authentication": "headerAuth",
        "headerParametersJson": "={\"Authorization\":\"Bearer \"+$env.SENDGRID_API_KEY}",
        "jsonParameters": true,
        "bodyParametersJson": "={\"personalizations\":[{\"to\":[{\"email\":$json.payload.user_email||\"\"}],\"subject\":\"We received your request\"}],\"from\":{\"email\":$env.ALERT_EMAIL_FROM},\"content\":[{\"type\":\"text/plain\",\"value\":\"Hi,\\n\\nWe received your request and created ticket \"+$json.payload.ticket_id+\".\\nWe’ll get back to you as soon as possible.\\n\\n— PureTask Support\"}]}"
      }
    }
  ],
  "connections": {
    "Events Webhook (Support)": { "main": [[{ "node": "Filter support.ticket.created", "type": "main", "index": 0 }]] },
    "Filter support.ticket.created": { "main": [[{ "node": "Slack: New Support Ticket", "type": "main", "index": 0 }, { "node": "Email: Ticket Confirmation (User)", "type": "main", "index": 0 }]] }

  "active": false

3️⃣ PT_Support_TicketSlaBreachReminder
Cron + backend query
Goal: remind when tickets are approaching or past SLA.

Assumed endpoint:
GET https://backend.yourdomain.com/internal/support/sla-breaches?min_minutes_open=240

Returns array of tickets with minutes_open, priority, routed_to.

{
  "name": "PT_Support_TicketSlaBreachReminder",
  "nodes": [
    { "id": "Cron", "name": "Every 1 hour", "type": "n8n-nodes-base.cron", "typeVersion": 1, "position": [260, 300], "parameters": { "triggerTimes": [{ "hour": 0, "minute": 0 }], "interval": 1, "unit": "hours" } },
    { "id": "Get", "name": "Backend: SLA Breaches", "type": "n8n-nodes-base.httpRequest", "typeVersion": 1, "position": [520, 300], "parameters": { "url": "https://backend.yourdomain.com/internal/support/sla-breaches?min_minutes_open=240", "method": "GET", "jsonParameters": true } },
    { "id": "Split", "name": "Split Tickets", "type": "n8n-nodes-base.itemLists", "typeVersion": 1, "position": [780, 300], "parameters": { "operation": "splitItems" } },
    {
      "id": "Slack",
      "name": "Slack: SLA Reminder",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.httpRequest",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [1040, 300],
      "parameters": {
        "url": "={{$env.ALERT_SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL}}",
        "method": "POST",
        "jsonParameters": true,
        "bodyParametersJson": "={\"text\":\"⏱️ SLA reminder\\nTicket: `\"+$json.ticket_id+\"`\\nPriority: \"+($json.priority||\"normal\")+\"\\nQueue: \"+($json.routed_to||\"support\")+\"\\nOpen: \"+($json.minutes_open||0)+\" minutes\"}"
      }
    }
  ],

1️⃣ PT_Monitoring_HealthCheck_Watchdog
Cron pings /health; alerts Slack if unhealthy.

{
  "name": "PT_Monitoring_HealthCheck_Watchdog",
  "nodes": [
    { "id": "Cron", "name": "Every 5 minutes", "type": "n8n-nodes-base.cron", "typeVersion": 1, "position": [260, 300], "parameters": { "triggerTimes": [{ "hour": 0, "minute": 0 }], "interval": 5, "unit": "minutes" } },
    { "id": "Ping", "name": "Backend: Health Check", "type": "n8n-nodes-base.httpRequest", "typeVersion": 1, "position": [520, 300], "parameters": { "url": "https://backend.yourdomain.com/health", "method": "GET", "jsonParameters": true, "options": { "timeout": 8000 } } },
    {
      "id": "If",
      "name": "If unhealthy",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.if",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [780, 300],
      "parameters": {
        "conditions": { "boolean": [{ "value1": "={{$json.ok}}", "operation": "isFalse" }] }
      }
    },
    {
      "id": "Slack",
      "name": "Slack: Health Alert",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.httpRequest",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [1040, 300],
      "parameters": {
        "url": "={{$env.ALERT_SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL}}",
        "method": "POST",
        "jsonParameters": true,
        "bodyParametersJson": "={\"text\":\"🚨 Backend health check FAILED. Response: \"+JSON.stringify($json)}"
      }
    }
  ],
  "connections": {
    "Every 5 minutes": { "main": [[{ "node": "Backend: Health Check", "type": "main", "index": 0 }]] },
    "Backend: Health Check": { "main": [[{ "node": "If unhealthy", "type": "main", "index": 0 }]] },
    "If unhealthy": { "main": [[{ "node": "Slack: Health Alert", "type": "main", "index": 0 }]] }
  },
  "active": false
}
If your /health returns { "status": "ok" } instead of { "ok": true }, swap the IF condition to check that.

    { "id": "Cron", "name": "Daily 08:30", "type": "n8n-nodes-base.cron", "typeVersion": 1, "position": [260, 300], "parameters": { "triggerTimes": [{ "hour": 8, "minute": 30 }] } },

      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [780, 300],

      }
    },
    {

      }

1️⃣ PT_Stripe_PaymentIntentSucceeded

Next Family — Matching / Assignment & Availability Automations (Option A: n8n JSON)
This family is everything around: job offers, wave releases, acceptance reminders, offer expirations, “no candidates” escalation, availability gap alerts, reassignment notifications.

Delivering 9 workflows:

PT_Assignment_WaveReleased_NotifyEligibleCleaners

PT_Assignment_OfferSent_NotifyCleaner

PT_Assignment_OfferReminder_15m

PT_Assignment_OfferExpired_NotifyClientOps

PT_Assignment_NoCandidatesFound_AlertOps

PT_Assignment_JobAccepted_NotifyClient

PT_Assignment_JobDeclined_TrackAndAlertIfLowFlex

PT_Assignment_Reassignment_NotifyParties

PT_Availability_GapAlert_UpcomingDemand

Assumed model: backend emits events + exposes a couple “internal” endpoints for batch reminder queries.

Next Family — Job Lifecycle Execution Automations (Option A: n8n JSON)
This family covers: pre-job reminders, check-in gating nudges, in-progress guardrails, photo compliance prompts, completion/approval reminders, dispute-window countdown, and post-job “receipt” messaging.

Next Family — Fraud / Trust & Safety Automations (Option A: n8n JSON)
This family is for risk escalations, pattern flags, payout safety escalations, manual review queues, and rapid ops alerts. Backend should compute the scores + set flags; n8n is the routing + alerting layer.

1️⃣ PT_Trust_ClientRiskBandChanged_Alert
Event: client_risk.band.changed
Goal: when a client enters High/Critical, alert trust_safety/ops.

{
  "name": "PT_Trust_ClientRiskBandChanged_Alert",
  "nodes": [
    { "id": "Webhook", "name": "Events Webhook (Client Risk)", "type": "n8n-nodes-base.webhook", "typeVersion": 1, "position": [260, 300], "parameters": { "httpMethod": "POST", "path": "events-client-risk-band-changed" } },
    { "id": "If", "name": "Filter client_risk.band.changed", "type": "n8n-nodes-base.if", "typeVersion": 1, "position": [520, 300], "parameters": { "conditions": { "string": [{ "value1": "={{$json.event_name}}", "operation": "equal", "value2": "client_risk.band.changed" }] } } },
    {
      "id": "IfHigh",
      "name": "If High/Critical",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.if",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [780, 300],
      "parameters": {
        "conditions": {
          "multi": [
            { "conditions": { "string": [{ "value1": "={{$json.payload.new_band}}", "operation": "equal", "value2": "High" }] } },
            { "conditions": { "string": [{ "value1": "={{$json.payload.new_band}}", "operation": "equal", "value2": "Critical" }] } }
          ],
          "combineOperation": "any"
        }
      }
    },
    {
      "id": "Slack",
      "name": "Slack: High Risk Client Alert",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.httpRequest",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [1040, 300],
      "parameters": {
        "url": "={{$env.ALERT_SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL}}",
        "method": "POST",
        "jsonParameters": true,
        "bodyParametersJson": "={\"text\":\"🛡️ Client risk escalated\\nClient: `\"+$json.payload.client_id+\"`\\nBand: *\"+$json.payload.old_band+\" → \"+$json.payload.new_band+\"*\\nScore: \"+($json.payload.score||\"?\")+\"\\nReason: \"+($json.payload.reason||\"(none)\")}"
      }
    }
  ],
  "connections": {
    "Events Webhook (Client Risk)": { "main": [[{ "node": "Filter client_risk.band.changed", "type": "main", "index": 0 }]] },
    "Filter client_risk.band.changed": { "main": [[{ "node": "If High/Critical", "type": "main", "index": 0 }]] },
    "If High/Critical": { "main": [[{ "node": "Slack: High Risk Client Alert", "type": "main", "index": 0 }]] }
  },
  "active": false

⏳ B) Reschedule / Cancellation / No-Show communications layer
Backend logic exists, but n8n should handle human comms + escalation:

Cancellation initiated → notify other party + ops if late

Reschedule requested → notify other party, reminders to respond, auto-expire

No-show detected → notify, open ticket, trigger compensation messaging

“Lock window” violations → friendly education email + log

⏳ C) Cleaner onboarding & compliance automation

Welcome sequence (Day 0/1/3)

Required docs missing (ID, W9/1099 prompt if needed)

First-job coaching sequence

Tier education + “how to reach Elite” nudges

Referral code created → send share kit

Abandoned checkout (credits)

Post-job review request + share link

⏳ E) Premium features (boosts / subscriptions / rush jobs)
Backend mentions boosts/subscriptions. n8n should do:

Boost started/expired notifications

Subscription failed payment → user + ops

Rush job created → special broadcast logic

Upsell sequences based on behavior

⏳ F) Data exports / accounting / compliance ops
You’ve got reconciliation + ledger integrity, but finance will still want:

Monthly export to CSV (payouts, refunds, revenue, fees)

Tax prep exports (cleaner earnings)

Chargeback evidence reminders + checklist

Important reality check: “Finished” vs “import-ready”

Several workflows assume internal endpoints like /internal/jobs/... and /admin/monitoring/....
If those endpoints don’t exist yet, then what’s “left” is adding those query endpoints OR rewriting those workflows to query Neon directly (via n8n Postgres node).

✅ Support & Messaging Family — Covered
If you want, the next family should be Cancellation / Reschedule / No-Show communications (because backend already has the logic; n8n adds “humans + messaging + escalation”).

Say “proceed” and I’ll generate that next in Option A JSON.


proceed

Proceeding ✅

Next Family — Cancellation / Reschedule / No-Show Communications & Escalations (Option A: n8n JSON)
This family is the “communications wrapper” around backend policy engines:

Reschedule requests → notify, remind, auto-expire, escalate

Cancellations → notify other party, late-cancel escalation, policy education

No-shows → instant ops ticket + compensation messaging + follow-ups

Lock-window / grace / fees → clear messaging and audit

Delivering 12 workflows:

PT_Reschedule_RequestCreated_NotifyOtherParty

PT_Reschedule_RequestReminder_Respond

PT_Reschedule_RequestExpired_NotifyAndEscalate

PT_Reschedule_Accepted_NotifyBoth

PT_Reschedule_Declined_NotifyRequester

PT_Cancel_Initiated_NotifyOtherParty

PT_Cancel_LateCancel_EscalateOps

PT_Cancel_Processed_SendReceipt

PT_Cancel_LockWindowBlocked_ExplainPolicy

PT_NoShow_Detected_NotifyAndOpenTicket

PT_NoShow_CompensationGranted_Notify

PT_CancelReschedule_DailyDigest

Assumes events emitted by backend:

reschedule.request.created|accepted|declined|expired

cancellation.initiated|processed|blocked.lock_window

job.no_show.detected

compensation.granted

1️⃣ PT_Reschedule_RequestCreated_NotifyOtherParty
Event: reschedule.request.created

  "name": "PT_Reschedule_RequestCreated_NotifyOtherParty",

Premium Features (Boosts / Rush Jobs / Subscriptions lifecycle)

boost purchased → activate + notify

boost expiring → reminder

boost expired → notify

rush job created → special broadcast waves

Proceeding ✅

Next Family — Premium Features (Boosts / Rush Jobs / Subscriptions Lifecycle) (Option A: n8n JSON)
This family covers:

Cleaner Boosts (purchase → activate → expire → reminders)

Rush Jobs (created → special broadcast + ops alert)

Subscriptions (created → welcome → renewal → cancellation → winback)

Dunning (already partly covered in Growth; here we add “retry + final notice + cancel flow”)

Delivering 12 workflows:

PT_Premium_BoostPurchased_ActivateAndNotify

PT_Premium_BoostExpiringSoon_RemindCleaner

PT_Premium_BoostExpired_NotifyCleaner

PT_Premium_RushJobCreated_BroadcastWave

PT_Premium_RushJobNoCandidates_EscalateOps

PT_Premium_SubscriptionCreated_Welcome

PT_Premium_SubscriptionRenewed_Receipt

PT_Premium_SubscriptionPaymentFailed_RetrySequence

PT_Premium_SubscriptionCanceled_ConfirmAndWinback

PT_Premium_SubscriptionPaused_Explain

PT_Premium_ReferralBoostApplied_NotifyCleaner

PT_Premium_WeeklyPremiumDigest

Assumed backend events:

boost.purchased, boost.expiring_soon, boost.expired

rush_job.created, rush_job.no_candidates

subscription.created, subscription.renewed, subscription.payment_failed, subscription.canceled, subscription.paused

boost.applied.referral (optional)
And internal endpoints:

/internal/premium/boosts-expiring?minutes=180

/admin/premium/weekly-digest

Option D: One master n8n map showing every event → workflow → side effect

Got it — here’s Option D: the master n8n map that shows every event → workflow → side effect (notifications, ops alerts, backend calls, exports, etc.).

I’m going to present it in 3 layers so it’s readable and implementation-ready:

Event Bus (single entry) → routes by event_name

Workflows grouped by family

Side effects (SendGrid / Slack / Backend calls / Tickets / Exports)

Master Event Router Concept (how everything connects)
ONE inbound webhook in n8n:

POST /events (from your backend event publisher)

Switch on event_name

Forward to the correct “family workflow” (or directly process)

This prevents having 50 different webhook URLs and makes the system easier to operate.

Master Map (Mermaid)
Copy/paste into any Mermaid renderer (GitHub, Notion, Mermaid Live) to visualize.




Event → Workflow → Side Effects (canonical list)
A) Job + Matching
job.created → Job Creation Workflow → notify cleaner candidates + schedule tracking + audit

job.assigned → Assignment/Offer → send offers (push/email) + update offer tables

job.accepted → Acceptance notify → notify client + lock assignment

job.in_progress → Tracking/Check-in → push reminders + ops alert if check-in missing

job.approved → Completion → release escrow/ledger finalize + ask for reviews (Growth)

B) Reschedule / Cancel / No-show
reschedule.request.created → notify other party (SendGrid)

reschedule.request.accepted → notify both

reschedule.request.declined → notify requester

reschedule.request.expired → notify requester + Slack ops

cancellation.initiated → notify other party

cancellation.processed → send receipt + if late/high inconvenience → Slack escalation

cancellation.blocked.lock_window → policy email

job.no_show.detected → create ticket + notify + Slack ops

compensation.granted → notify user (credits/refund/bonus)

C) Payments / Stripe / Payouts / Reconciliation
stripe.event.received → Stripe Router → idempotency tables → call correct backend processors

checkout.abandoned → 1h + 24h recovery emails

payouts.paused → email cleaner with resolution steps

recon.mismatch → Slack urgent (and backend auto-pause already)

D) Cleaner onboarding / compliance
cleaner.created → welcome email

background_check.status.changed → update email

cleaner.docs.missing → reminders (cron + query)

reliability.tier.changed → tier explanation + how-to-improve

E) Growth / referrals / reviews
referral.code.created → share kit

referral.invite.sent → internal log + optional reminders

referral.converted → notify rewards issued

referral.reward.failed → Slack escalation

job.approved → review requests (client + cleaner)

F) Premium
boost.purchased → backend activate + email

boost.expiring_soon → reminder

boost.expired → ended email

rush_job.created → backend broadcast + ops alert

rush_job.no_candidates → ops escalation

subscription.created → welcome

subscription.renewed → receipt

subscription.payment_failed → retry cadence (Day 0/2/5)

subscription.canceled → confirm + 7-day winback

subscription.paused → explain

G) Compliance / exports / integrity (Cron)
Monthly exports → SendGrid to finance

Daily ledger integrity → Slack on fail

Daily orphaned stripe objects → Slack warn

Weekly digests → Slack summaries (growth/premium/finance/ops)

What this “master map” looks like in n8n (implementation shape)
You’ll have:

Workflow 0: PT_Master_EventRouter

Webhook /events

Verify HMAC secret

Switch on event_name

Execute Workflow node for each matching workflow (or route to sub-workflow)

Family workflows (what we’ve been building)

Accept standardized payload {event_name, event_id, created_at, payload:{...}}

Side effects: SendGrid, Slack, backend calls, ticket creation, etc.

Cron workflows

Pull lists via backend endpoints

Split in batches

Notify / export / alert

Next step (no questions, just action)
If you want, I can output the single “PT_Master_EventRouter” workflow JSON that contains:

One webhook (/events)

HMAC verification

Switch router with all event names

Execute Workflow nodes pointing to every workflow we created

Just say: “generate PT_Master_EventRouter JSON” and I’ll drop it in import-ready format.

{
  "name": "PT_Master_EventRouter",
  "nodes": [
    {

        "httpMethod": "POST",
        "path": "events",
        "responseMode": "onReceived",
        "options": {}
      },
      "id": "pt_webhook_events",
      "name": "Webhook: /events",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.webhook",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [260, 360]
    },
    {
      "parameters": {
        "functionCode": "const crypto = require('crypto');\n\n// Expected inbound shape:\n// {\n//   event_id: \"evt_...\",\n//   event_name: \"...\",\n//   created_at: \"...\",\n//   payload: {...}\n// }\n\n// HMAC verification (optional but strongly recommended)\n// Backend should send header: x-pt-signature = HMAC_SHA256(rawBody, N8N_WEBHOOK_SECRET)\n// If you can't provide rawBody in your n8n setup, you can disable signature check by setting PT_VERIFY_HMAC=false.\n\nconst verify = (process.env.PT_VERIFY_HMAC || 'true').toLowerCase() !== 'false';\n\n// n8n provides headers on $json? No. Use $headers.\nconst headers = $headers || {};\nconst sig = headers['x-pt-signature'] || headers['X-PT-Signature'] || headers['x-pt-signature'.toLowerCase()];\n\nif (verify) {\n  const secret = process.env.N8N_WEBHOOK_SECRET;\n  if (!secret) throw new Error('Missing N8N_WEBHOOK_SECRET');\n  if (!sig) throw new Error('Missing x-pt-signature header');\n\n  // Best-effort raw body: in many n8n deployments, raw body is not directly accessible in Function node.\n  // If your instance supports it, the webhook node can be configured to keep raw body.\n  // Fallback: sign the canonical JSON string.\n  const canonical = JSON.stringify($json);\n  const expected = crypto.createHmac('sha256', secret).update(canonical).digest('hex');\n  if (sig !== expected) {\n    throw new Error('Invalid signature');\n  }\n}\n\n// Normalize event_name\nconst event_name = ($json.event_name || '').trim();\nif (!event_name) throw new Error('Missing event_name');\n\nreturn [{ json: { ...$json, event_name } }];"

Quick wiring notes (so this imports cleanly)
Replace every REPLACE_WITH_WORKFLOW_ID_... with the actual workflowId from n8n.

If you prefer names instead of IDs: keep IDs, but you can also route via Execute Workflow node picker after import.

If you want true HMAC over the raw HTTP body, enable “Raw Body” in webhook settings (varies by n8n deployment). Otherwise the “canonical JSON HMAC” fallback works as long as backend signs the same JSON string.

If you say “add default route to Slack for unknown events”, I’ll patch the router so any unmatched event_name gets logged and still returns 200.


wat workflows out of the ones we have created are the most important . which workflow should i create and implement first, second, third ,ect

Here’s the exact order I’d implement the n8n workflows in for PureTask — based on risk + money protection + marketplace stability + ops load.

If you do these in this order, you get a backend that’s not just “working”, but safe to launch.

Phase 1 — “Don’t lose money / Don’t break trust” (do first)
These are the workflows that prevent financial disasters, broken payments, and angry users.

PT_Master_EventRouter

Everything depends on this. If events don’t route cleanly, nothing else triggers reliably.

Stripe Router (Idempotency) — stripe.event.received → Stripe workflow

Prevents duplicate credits, duplicate payouts, duplicate refunds.

This is your #1 “financial correctness” safeguard.

Payout Weekly + Payout Retry + Payout Pause (flagged cleaners)

Ensures cleaners get paid reliably and you can stop payouts instantly if fraud/flags.

Recon Mismatch Alert (recon.mismatch) + AutoPausePayouts worker

If earnings ≠ payouts, you must know immediately. This catches silent leakage.

Cancellation Processed Receipt + Escalation

This touches credits, refunds, and compensation. Must be correct early.

Phase 2 — “Marketplace must function” (do second)
These keep jobs flowing and prevent churn.

Job Assigned / Offer Broadcast

Without this, no one gets jobs → marketplace dead.

Job Accepted Notify (client + cleaner)

Reduces no-shows and confusion.

Job In-Progress Guardrails (check-in, photos, tracking)

Protects quality + stops disputes. Also drives reliability scoring properly.

Job Approved (completion) + Review requests

Completion triggers escrow release + earnings + reviews. Critical loop.

No-Show Detected → Ticket + Notify + Bonus/Refund logic

One of the most common “this app is broken” moments if you don’t automate it.

Phase 3 — “Reduce support load / prevent chaos” (do third)
These stop endless manual handling.

Reschedule Request Created / Accepted / Declined / Expired

Reschedules create massive support load if not automated.

Cancel Lock Window policy messaging (cancellation.blocked.lock_window)

Prevents rage/support tickets.

Compensation Granted Notify

Users must be told immediately when credits/bonuses are added (trust).

Phase 4 — “Activation + retention” (do fourth)
These drive cleaner supply and client retention after core stability is proven.

Cleaner Welcome D0

Stripe Connect incomplete nudges (D1/D3)

Missing docs reminder

Background check status updates

Tier changed education

If supply is weak, do these earlier.

Phase 5 — “Growth & premium” (do fifth)
These are powerful but not required for a stable launch.

Abandoned checkout recovery (1h + 24h)

Referral code created share kit

Referral converted reward notify

Boost purchased activate + notify

Rush job broadcast + no candidates escalation

Subscription lifecycle (created/renewed/failed/canceled)

Phase 6 — “Finance exports / audit / compliance” (do last)
Important, but not required for day-1 survival.

Monthly payouts export

Monthly refunds/chargebacks export

Revenue/fee recon export

Daily ledger integrity check

Orphaned stripe objects check

Weekly finance digest

The Top 10 “Launch-Critical” workflows (if you only do 10)
PT_Master_EventRouter

Stripe Router (Idempotency)

Payout Weekly

Payout Retry

Recon Mismatch Alert

Job Offer / Assignment Broadcast

Job Accepted Notify

Job In-Progress Guardrails

Job Approved / Completion

Cancellation Processed (credits/refunds) + receipt

What I need from you to turn this into a clean “implementation checklist”
Tell me which mode you want next:

Mode 1: “I’m launching in 7 days” → I’ll give a hard top-10 checklist + test cases for each.

Mode 2: “I’m still building” → I’ll give a dependency tree + what endpoints/events must exist before each workflow can run.

Just reply Mode 1 or Mode 2.

Yep — below are import-ready n8n workflow JSONs for the 4 “launch-critical” workflows you listed.

Notes (applies to all):

Replace https://backend.yourdomain.com with your backend base URL.

These assume the inbound payload shape from your backend event system is:

{
  "event_id": "evt_123",
  "event_name": "stripe.event.received",
  "created_at": "2025-01-01T00:00:00Z",
  "payload": { ... }
}
These use env vars you already referenced:

N8N_WEBHOOK_SECRET

ALERT_SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL

SENDGRID_API_KEY

ALERT_EMAIL_FROM

ALERT_EMAIL_TO

1) Stripe Router (Idempotency)
Workflow: PT_Stripe_Router_Idempotent
Trigger: called by PT_Master_EventRouter via Execute Workflow (recommended)
Purpose: route Stripe events safely to backend processors; backend handles idempotency via stripe_events + stripe_object_processed.

{
  "name": "PT_Stripe_Router_Idempotent",
  "nodes": [
    {
      "id": "in",
      "name": "Input (from master router)",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.noOp",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [260, 300],
      "parameters": {}
    },
    {
      "id": "if",
      "name": "Filter stripe.event.received",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.if",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [520, 300],
      "parameters": {
        "conditions": {
          "string": [
            {
              "value1": "={{$json.event_name}}",
              "operation": "equal",
              "value2": "stripe.event.received"
            }
          ]
        }
      }
    },
    {
      "id": "call",
      "name": "Backend: Process Stripe Event (Idempotent)",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.httpRequest",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [800, 300],
      "parameters": {
        "url": "https://backend.yourdomain.com/stripe/events/process",
        "method": "POST",
        "jsonParameters": true,
        "bodyParametersJson": "={{$json.payload}}",
        "options": {
          "timeout": 60000
        }
      }
    },
    {
      "id": "slack",
      "name": "Slack: Stripe Processing Failed",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.httpRequest",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [800, 460],
      "parameters": {
        "url": "={{$env.ALERT_SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL}}",
        "method": "POST",
        "jsonParameters": true,
        "bodyParametersJson": "={\"text\":\"🚨 Stripe event processing FAILED\\nEvent: `\"+($json.event_id||\"?\")+\"`\\nType: \"+($json.payload?.type||\"?\")}"
      }
    }
  ],
  "connections": {
    "Input (from master router)": {
      "main": [
        [
          {
            "node": "Filter stripe.event.received",
            "type": "main",
            "index": 0
          }
        ]
      ]
    },
    "Filter stripe.event.received": {
      "main": [
        [
          {
            "node": "Backend: Process Stripe Event (Idempotent)",
            "type": "main",
            "index": 0
          }
        ],
        [
          {
            "node": "Slack: Stripe Processing Failed",
            "type": "main",
            "index": 0
          }
        ]
      ]
    }
  },
  "active": false,
  "settings": {
    "executionTimeout": 300,
    "saveExecutionProgress": true,
    "saveDataErrorExecution": "all",
    "saveDataSuccessExecution": "none"
  },
  "versionId": "pt-stripe-router-v1"
}
✅ This design is intentionally “thin”: n8n routes; backend enforces idempotency and financial correctness.

2) Payout Weekly + Payout Retry + Payout Pause
2a) Weekly Payout Processor
Workflow: PT_Payouts_Weekly_Run
Trigger: Cron weekly
Purpose: call backend weekly payout batch (Stripe Connect transfers + ledger updates).

{
  "name": "PT_Payouts_Weekly_Run",
  "nodes": [
    {
      "id": "cron",
      "name": "Cron: Weekly (Mon 03:00)",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.cron",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [260, 300],
      "parameters": {
        "triggerTimes": [
          {
            "dayOfWeek": "1",
            "hour": 3,
            "minute": 0
          }
        ]
      }
    },
    {
      "id": "run",
      "name": "Backend: Run Weekly Payouts",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.httpRequest",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [520, 300],
      "parameters": {
        "url": "https://backend.yourdomain.com/payouts/run-weekly",
        "method": "POST",
        "jsonParameters": true,
        "bodyParametersJson": "={\"source\":\"n8n\",\"run_at\":new Date().toISOString()}",
        "options": { "timeout": 120000 }
      }
    },
    {
      "id": "slackOk",
      "name": "Slack: Weekly Payouts Started",
      "type": "n8n-nodes-base.httpRequest",
      "typeVersion": 1,
      "position": [780, 300],
      "parameters": {
        "url": "={{$env.ALERT_SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL}}",
        "method": "POST",
        "jsonParameters": true,
        "bodyParametersJson": "={\"text\":\"💸 Weekly payouts started (backend batch triggered).\"}"
      }
    }
  ],
  "connections": {
    "Cron: Weekly (Mon 03:00)": {
      "main": [[{ "node": "Backend: Run Weekly Payouts", "type": "main", "index": 0 }]]
    },
    "Backend: Run Weekly Payouts": {

4) Cancellation Processed Receipt + Escalation

Your backend should emit these events after it has already done the ledger-critical action, for example:

cancellation.processed should include final deltas and fee percent after the ledger entries are committed.

recon.mismatch should include flag_id, expected, actual, and confirm the backend already paused payouts.

how do i import jsons into n8n

Great question — this is very straightforward, but there are a couple of gotchas that are worth knowing so you don’t get stuck.

Below is the exact, safe way to import the JSON workflows I gave you into n8n.

✅ How to Import JSON Workflows into n8n
Method 1 (RECOMMENDED): Import via UI
This is the cleanest and safest way.

Step-by-step
Open n8n

Go to your n8n dashboard (cloud or self-hosted).

Go to the Workflows page

Left sidebar → Workflows

Click “Import”

Top-right corner → Import from file
(or “Import workflow” depending on version)

Paste or upload JSON

You can:

Upload the .json file

OR paste the entire JSON directly

Confirm

Click Import

The workflow will appear in Draft (inactive) state

Save

Open the workflow

Click Save

That’s it ✅

Method 2: Paste Directly into a New Workflow
Useful when you’re moving fast.

Click “New Workflow”

Top-right → ⋮ menu

Select Import from clipboard

Paste the JSON

Save

🚨 Critical Post-Import Checklist (DO NOT SKIP)
After importing each workflow, you must do these:

1️⃣ Replace Placeholder Workflow IDs
In workflows like PT_Master_EventRouter:

Find nodes named:

Exec: ...
Replace:

REPLACE_WITH_WORKFLOW_ID_...
With the actual workflow ID from n8n
(click workflow → Settings → ID)

💡 Tip: Do this after importing all sub-workflows.

2️⃣ Set Environment Variables
Make sure these exist in n8n:

Variable	Required
N8N_WEBHOOK_SECRET	✅
ALERT_SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL	✅
SENDGRID_API_KEY	✅
ALERT_EMAIL_FROM	✅
ALERT_EMAIL_TO	✅
If missing → workflows will fail silently.

3️⃣ Verify Webhook URLs
For workflows with Webhook nodes:

Open the node

Copy the Production URL

Make sure your backend sends events to that URL

Example:

POST https://n8n.yourdomain.com/webhook/events
4️⃣ Leave Workflows INACTIVE First
🚫 Do not activate everything immediately.

Correct order:

Import workflows

Wire IDs in Master Router

Send test events (see below)

Confirm Slack / Email fires

Activate

🧪 How to Test After Import (VERY IMPORTANT)
Test Event (example)
Send this from Postman / curl:

POST /webhook/events
{
  "event_id": "test_evt_1",
  "event_name": "recon.mismatch",
  "created_at": "2025-01-01T00:00:00Z",
  "payload": {
    "cleaner_id": "cleaner_123",
    "expected": 12000,
    "actual": 11800,
    "flag_id": "flag_999"
  }
}
Expected result:

Slack alert fires

Workflow execution shows green check

Response = { ok: true, routed: true }

🧠 Best Practice (Strongly Recommended)
Name & tag workflows consistently
Example:

PT / Payments / Stripe Router
PT / Payouts / Weekly Run
PT / Payouts / Retry
PT / Finance / Recon Alert
PT / Jobs / Cancellation Processed
This keeps ops sane once you have 40+ workflows.

                  can u import multiple workflows at once?                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       

Yes — you can import multiple workflows at once in n8n, but how you do it matters. Here’s the clear, no-BS breakdown.

✅ Can you import multiple workflows at once?
YES — in two supported ways
NO — not directly via the UI one-by-one import
Let’s go through the correct options, ranked best → worst.

🥇 BEST OPTION: Import a single JSON file containing multiple workflows
This is how teams actually do it.

How it works
n8n supports bulk import if the JSON file contains an array of workflows

Each workflow is its own object inside the array

Structure example
[
  { "name": "PT_Stripe_Router_Idempotent", ... },
  { "name": "PT_Payouts_Weekly_Run", ... },
  { "name": "PT_Payouts_Retry_Failed", ... },
  { "name": "PT_Recon_Mismatch_Alert", ... },
  { "name": "PT_Cancellation_Processed_Receipt_Escalation", ... }
]
How to import
Workflows → Import from file

Upload the single JSON file

n8n will create ALL workflows at once

All will be inactive drafts

✅ This is the cleanest and safest approach
✅ Perfect for your current stage (many workflows)

If you want, I can bundle all workflows we’ve created into one bulk-import JSON.

🥈 SECOND BEST: n8n CLI (self-hosted only)
If you’re running n8n on your own server.

n8n import:workflow --input=./workflows/
Imports all JSON files in a directory

Preserves names and IDs

Ideal for version control (Git)

❌ Not available on n8n Cloud
❌ Requires CLI access

🥉 OK BUT MANUAL: Import one-by-one in UI
This is what you already know.

Works

Slow

Easy to mess up ordering

Not scalable past ~10 workflows

🚫 What you CANNOT do
You cannot select multiple JSON files in the UI and import them together

You cannot copy/paste multiple workflows unless they’re wrapped in an array

⚠️ VERY IMPORTANT GOTCHAS (read this)
1️⃣ Workflow IDs will change
After bulk import, workflow IDs are regenerated

You must re-wire:

Execute Workflow nodes

PT_Master_EventRouter

This is expected and normal.

2️⃣ Activate AFTER wiring
Correct order:

Import all workflows

Copy workflow IDs

Update Master Router

Test with fake events

Activate

3️⃣ Environment variables must exist FIRST
Otherwise imports succeed but executions fail silently.

✅ What I recommend for you (100%)
Do this next:
Let me bundle all launch-critical workflows into one bulk JSON

Import once

Wire Master Router

Test 5 events

Go live

If you want that bundle, just say:

“Bundle the launch-critical workflows into one JSON for import.”

I’ll generate it cleanly.
